===
Ternary If Precedence Abuse
===

begin
  Result := A + if B then C else D * E;
  (if A then ObjA else ObjB).DoSomething;
  if A then if B then C else D else E;
end;

          (kAdd)
          (exprIf

            (identifier)
            (kThen)
            (identifier)
            (kElse)
            (exprBinary
              (identifier)
              (kMul)
              (identifier)))))
      (statement
        (exprDot
          (exprParens
            (exprIf
              (kIf)
              (identifier)
              (kThen)
              (identifier)
              (kElse)
              (identifier)))
          (kDot)
          (identifier)))

        (kIf)
        (identifier)
        (kThen)
        (ifElse
